--- Commit Message ---
LU-14160 fallocate: Add punch mode to fallocate

This patch adds fallocate(2) punch operation
(FALLOCATE_FL_PUNCH_HOLE) mode support for ldiskfs backend
OSD and for OSC/OST

Test cases sanity/150{f,g} are added for verification.
FSX test was modified:
 - add 'punch' operation to an output
 - fix 'No space' problem when fallocate length become negative
 - fix wrong bytes number in output

Test-Parameters: testlist=sanity ostsizegb=12 env=ONLY="150f 150g"
Signed-off-by: Arshad Hussain <arshad.hussain@aeoncomputing.com>

Thanks for the patch.

Patch Set 2: Code-Review-1

(2 comments)

the logic in cl_falloc() about sa_falloc_end checking is not clear, could you explain why checks were changed for FL_PUNCH_HOLE what it checks exactly?
Also logic is based on FL_KEEP_SIZE existence rather than FL_PUNCH_HOLE but I'd expect otherwise considering that new changes are caused by  introduction. While FL_PUNCH_HOLE must be combined with FL_KEEP_SIZE the latter could be used alone as well

# MOUNT_2="yes" bash ./lustre/tests/llmount.sh
# bash ./fsxtest2.sh
Starting fsx test
Run [1] started ...passed
Run [2] started ...passed
Run [3] started ...passed
Run [4] started ...passed
Run [5] started ...passed
Run [6] started ...passed
Run [7] started ...passed
Run [8] started ...passed
Run [9] started ...passed

#

fsxtest2.sh
~~~~~~~~~~~~~
#!/bin/bash

ret=100
testfile=fsxfile

# llmount.sh is already being called manually - MOUNT_2="yes" bash ./lustre/tests/llmount.sh
rm -f /mnt/lustre/${testfile}
rm -f /mnt/lustre2/${testfile}
lfs setstripe -c -1 /mnt/lustre/${testfile}

echo "Starting fsx test"
for run in {1..90}
do
	echo -n "Run [$run] started ..."
	./lustre/tests/fsx -c 50 -p 100 -N 50000 -S 0 -l 10485760 /mnt/lustre/${testfile} /mnt/lustre2/${testfile} 2>/dev/null 1>&2
	ret=$?
	if [ $ret -ne 0 ]; then
		echo "failed"
		exit
	else
		echo "passed"
	fi

	# Refresh
	sleep 1
	rm -f /mnt/lustre/${testfile}
	rm -f /mnt/lustre2/${testfile}
	lfs setstripe -c -1 /mnt/lustre/${testfile}
done

echo "ALL PASS"
